[30;1m359 | [0m[35m    Basically, I try to prevent recording the time spent inside LineProfiler[0m
[30;1m360 | [0m[35m    doing all of the bookkeeping for each line. Each time Python's tracing[0m

[30;1m365 | [0m[35m    happens in between these two times.[0m
